sfex_jumpdrive_order_apply_cooldown_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOR = {
				has_global_flag = sfex_jumpdrive_order_global_flag_jump_drive_cooldown_disabled
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = sfex_jumpdrive_order_country_flag_jump_drive_cooldown_disabled
				}
				has_fleet_flag = sfex_jumpdrive_order_fleet_flag_jump_drive_cooldown_disabled
			}
		}
		sfex_core_create_global_country_if_needed = yes
		event_target:sfex_core_global_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_variable_set = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_sfex_jump_drive_cooldown_time
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_sfex_jump_drive_cooldown_time
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_variable_set = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_sfex_jump_drive_cooldown_time
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_sfex_jump_drive_cooldown_time
					value = event_target:sfex_core_global_country.sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_sfex_jump_drive_cooldown_time
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_ship = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = sfex_jump_drive_order_cooldown
				days = 1
				time_multiplier = owner.sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_sfex_jump_drive_cooldown_time
			}
		}
	}
}

sfex_jumpdrive_order_export_planets_in_system_distance_to_centre_point = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				exists = event_target:sfex_event_target_solar_system_centre_point
			}
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_star = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = sfex_event_target_solar_system_centre_point
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			exists = event_target:sfex_event_target_solar_system_centre_point
		}
		every_system_planet = {
			sfex_jumpdrive_order_measure_point_distance_to_centre_point = yes
		}
	}
	else = {
		log = "sfex_jumpdrive_order_export_distance_to_centre_point: is_primary_star does not exist."
	}
}

sfex_jumpdrive_order_measure_point_distance_to_centre_point = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			distance = {
				source = event_target:sfex_event_target_solar_system_centre_point
				min_distance >= 0
				max_distance <= 1
				same_solar_system = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
			value = 0
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			distance = {
				source = event_target:sfex_event_target_solar_system_centre_point
				min_distance >= 1
				max_distance <= 2

				source = event_target:sfex_event_target_solar_system_centre_point
				min_distance >= 481
				max_distance <= 482
				same_solar_system = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
			value = 481
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			distance = {
				source = event_target:sfex_event_target_solar_system_centre_point

sfex_jumpdrive_order_set_location = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_system_radius
				value = 0
			}
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
					value = 0
				}
			}
			prevprev = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 0
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {

		}

		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
					value = 0
				}
			}
			prevprev = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 496
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_system_radius
				value = 497
			}
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
					value = 0
				}
			}
			prevprev = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 497
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_system_radius
				value = 498
			}
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
					value = 0
				}
			}
			prevprev = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 498
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_system_radius
				value = 499
			}
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
					value = 0
				}
			}
			prevprev = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 499
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_system_radius
				value = 500
			}
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
					value = 0
				}
			}
			prevprev = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 500
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = sfex_jumpdrive_order_var_distance_measured
					value = 0
				}
			}
			prevprev = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 501					# Failsafe value.
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
